222.4(1): yin/ kan su'u mi rigs dpe skrun khang gi dbu khrid 'brug rgyal mkhar dang gcod pa 
222.5(1): rnam gnyis nas thugs khur rgyab skyor tshad med gnang ba dang / lhag par du dus rab 
222.6(1): kyi gnyan 'phrang mang po'i nang tshe srog 'ben dang bsdos te srung skyong byas pa'i dpe cha 
222.7(1): g.yar ba'i dpe bdag rnam pa dang / de bzhin nga tsho'i bstan don gyi bya ba kun la 
222.8(1): mthun sbyor gnang ba ma tshad dpe tshogs 'di dpar skrun skabs su yang ma bskul dang 
222.9(1): blang gis zhal 'debs gnang mkhan bcas dngos shugs brgyud gsum nas rgyu tshegs 
222.10(1): thabs gsum gyis sdong grogs rogs ram gnang mkhan yongs la snying dbus nas 
222.11(1): thugs rje che zhu rgyu dang / gsung rab dag bzhengs byas pa'i dge ba'i tshogs 'dis/
222.12(1): 7 skyabs rje rgyal ba sman ri ba'i mkhan slob rnam gnyis gtsos ris su ma chad pa'i 
222.13(1): bstan 'dzin skyes chen dam pa rnams kyi sku tshe bskal brgyar brtan zhing bzhed dgongs 
222.14(1): lhun gyis 'grub pa dang / 'brel thogs kyi sbyin pa'i bdag po dang las gzhi 'di'i byed 
222.15(1): po kun tshe bsod dbang khams gong nas gong du mtho ste myur du sku gsum rdzogs pa'i 
222.16(1): sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang thob pa dang / zhang bod rig gzhung rnams mi nyams gong nas 
222.17(1): gong du 'phel te 'dzam gling tha gru yongs kyi snod bcud rgud pa gso zhing phan bde'i 
222.18(1): gsos su khyab pa dang / yangs pa'i rgyal khams kun du nad mug 'khrug rtsod dang rang 
222.19(1): byung 'byung ba'i 'jigs pa rnams rmeng med du zhi nas bde legs phun tshogs skyid kyi nyi 
222.20(1): ma 'gro kun yongs la shar ba'i smon 'dun dang bcas 'byung ldan 3 1 spyi lo 2 15 5[ / ]1
222.21(1): nyin/ g.yung drung bon gyi bka' brten dpe rnying phyogs bsgrigs khang nas bris/ /
